Community Cup Battle for Zendikar Draft Decklists
=================================================



 Posted in [2015 MAGIC COMMUNITY CUP](/en/events/coverage/cc15)
 on September 20, 2015 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/person/wizards_authorpic_larger.jpg)
By Wizards of the Coast










Battle for Zendikar Booster Draft made its debut at the 2015 Community Cup! Check out what the Community and Wizards Teams drafted!
